##769 Characters

##West Africa##

#Basic characters to fill in history in tribal west africa. Giving them no dynasty since the game will auto give them a dynasty which works perfectly fine given none of the bookmark dynasty's for these titles are historical. Plus it also makes it so the oldest dynasty's in the world aren't made up tribal dynasty's
